style="font-size:20px;">Live Stream Saturday October 25th at 2:00 PM EDT of BWG Getting Dolled Up:<a href="http://www.twitch.tv/ocnbwg" target="_blank">http://www.twitch.tv/ocnbwg</a></span></strong></p> <p style="text-align:center;"></p> <p style="text-align:center;"></p> <p style="text-align:center;">By the powers vested in me, I hereby present:</p> <p style="text-align:center;"></p> <p style="text-align:center;"><a class="H-lightbox-open" href="http://www.overclock.net/content/type/61/id/2198101/"><img alt="" class="lightbox-enabled" data-id="2198101" data-type="61" src="http://www.overclock.net/content/type/61/id/2198101/width/1000/height/1000/flags/LL" style="; width: 1000px; height: 156px"></a></p> <p></p> <p></p> <p style="text-align:center;"><br><strong>----&gt;<a href="http://folding.axihub.ca/foldathon_signup.php" target="_blank">SIGN UP<span style="color:rgb(255,0,0);">HERE</span></a>&lt;----</strong><br><br><em>You only need to sign up 1 time. You'll always be in each event if you fold after signing up.</em></p> <div></div> <div> <p style="text-align:center;"></p> <p style="text-align:center;"></p> <p><strong>Points from October Foldathon (BWG gets all dolled up):</strong></p> <p><img alt="Foldathon Points" src="http://folding.axihub.ca/tmp/foldathon/points_foldathon_10_2014.png"></p> <div> <p></p> <p><strong>Points goal 2 from October Foldathon (Extra cash prizes):</strong></p> <p><img alt="Foldathon Points" src="http://folding.axihub.ca/tmp/foldathon/points2_foldathon_10_2014.png"></p> </div> </div> <p></p> <p><strong># Folders from</strong> <strong style="font-style:normal;">October</strong> <strong>Foldathon:</strong></p> <p><img alt="OCN Active Folders" src="http://folding.axihub.ca/tmp/foldathon/active_foldathon_10_2014.png"></p> <p></p> <p><strong><span style="text-decoration:underline;">What is the Foldathon?</span></strong><br><br> Every month we hold a Foldathon, or FAT for short. The FAT is a mad dash over a 2 day period where we fold on as much hardware as we can get a grubby fingers on and try toamass the most points possible. It is winner takes all. Okay,that's not true, butif you're lucky you might win something, probably not, but you will have made a honourable contribution to the science behind Folding@Home. What is that science you're probably asking, have a gander over<strong><a href="http://folding.stanford.edu/home/the-science" target="_blank">here</a></strong>to learn more.All units crunched for team 37726 count, even if you can only manage to complete one unit, but if you're already a folder, there's no excuse for not folding for the full 48 hours<img alt=":wubsmiley" src="http://files.overclock.net/images/smilies/wubsmiley.gif" style=""><br><br><br><br><strong><span style="text-decoration:underline;">How it works:</span></strong><br><br> Sign-up and run Folding@home for Overclock.net (team number: 37726) during the specified times. Those who Fold will be entered into a drawing to win the prizes listed below. If you still don't know what Folding@home is or need some help getting started, feel free to post here, make a thread in the<a href="http://www.overclock.net/f/55/overclock-net-folding-home-team">Overclock.net Folding@Home Team forum</a>or check this guide:<a href="http://www.overclock.net/t/977412/windows-7-complete-client-v7-guide">FAHControl v7 for both CPU and GPU</a></p> <p></p> <p></p> <p><a href="http://folding.axihub.ca/foldathon_signup.php" target="_blank"><strong>SIGN UP<span style="color:rgb(255,0,0);">HERE</span></strong></a>- If you have ever signed up for a FAT before today, then you are already signed up.</p> <p>Even if you go away for a couple months, you'll still be signed up. You can also verify whether or not you're signed up by looking for your name<strong><a href="http://folding.axihub.ca/foldathon.php" target="_blank">here</a></strong>in the member list.</p> <p></p> <p></p> <p></p> <p><strong><span style="text-decoration:underline;">When:</span></strong></p> <p></p> <p><strong>Monday</strong><strong style="font-style:normal;">October</strong><strong style="font-style:normal;">20th - Wednesday October22nd - starting and ending at 12:00 EDT / 16:00 UTC</strong></p> <p></p> <p><a href="http://www.timeanddate.com/worldclock/fixedtime.html?iso=20141020T1600&amp;p1=1440&amp;msg=October%202014%20Foldathon" target="_blank"><span style="color:rgb(0,128,0);"><strong>Countdown to start</strong></span></a></p> <p></p> <p><a href="http://www.timeanddate.com/worldclock/fixedtime.html?iso=20141022T1600&amp;p1=1440&amp;msg=October%202014%20Foldathon" target="_blank"><span style="color:rgb(255,0,0);"><strong>Countdown to end</strong></span></a><br><br><br><strong><span style="text-decoration:underline;">Reminders:</span></strong><br><br><strong>If you would like to be put on a reminder list for all future Foldathons, please join this group:<a href="http://www.overclock.net/groups/show/2194/foldathon-participants">Foldathon Participants</a></strong></p> <p></p> <p></p> <p><br><strong><span style="text-decoration:underline;">Prizes</span></strong><br><br><span style="text-decoration:underline;">OCN Donated:</span></p> <p></p> <p><strong>3x $25 PayPal</strong>- Deathclaw, lacrossewacker, Sethy666</p> <p><strong>2x Overclocked Accounts</strong> -
